/*!50003 CREATE*/ /*!50017 DEFINER=`root`@`%`*/ /*!50003 TRIGGER `daoju001`.`sync_comment_info`
AFTER INSERT ON `daoju001`.`t_comment`
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN 
  declare msgType int;
  declare senderType int;
  declare recType int;
  declare receiver int;
  declare qid int;
  declare count int;

  
  if(new.type) then
	select count(*) into count from t_comment cmt where cmt.parent = new.parent and cmt.type = 1;
    UPDATE t_professional_answer answer SET answer.cnt_comment = count where answer.id = new.parent;
  else
	select count(*) into count from t_comment cmt where cmt.parent = new.parent and cmt.type = 0;
	UPDATE t_question question SET question.cnt_CA = count where question.id = new.parent;
  end if;

  IF(NEW.type) then#解决方案中评论receiver是agent
	select agent_id,question_id into receiver,qid from t_professional_answer where id = NEW.parent;#查找发布问题的人
	if (senderType > 0) then
	  set msgType = 4;
	else
	  set msgType = 5;
	end if;
	IF (receiver != new.user_id) then
		INSERT into t_message SET answer_id = new.parent, sender_id = new.user_id, sender_name = NEW.user_name, receiver_id = receiver, type = msgType, question_id = qid, gmt_create = NEW.gmt_create;
	END IF;
  ELSE#问题中评论reciever是buyer
	select buyer_id into receiver from t_question where id = NEW.parent;#查找发布问题的人
	if (senderType > 0) then
	  set msgType = 2;
	else
	  set msgType = 3;
	end if;
	IF (receiver != new.user_id) then
		INSERT into t_message SET sender_id = new.user_id, sender_name = NEW.user_name, receiver_id = receiver, type = msgType, question_id = new.parent, gmt_create = NEW.gmt_create;
	END IF;
  END IF;

  #回复他人问题
  IF(NEW.comment_id) then
	select user_id into receiver from t_comment where id = NEW.comment_id;
	set recType = 1;
	if not(receiver != 0) then
	  select user_id into receiver from t_comment where id = NEW.comment_id;
	  set recType = 0;
	end if;
	if (recType > 0) then#receiver是agent
		if (senderType > 0) then
		  set msgType = 4;
		else
		  set msgType = 5;
		end if;
	else#receiver是buyer
		if (senderType > 0) then
		  set msgType = 2;
		else
		  set msgType = 3;
		end if;
	end if;
	if (NEW.type) then#解决方案中回复
	  INSERT into t_message SET answer_id = new.parent, sender_id = new.user_id, sender_name = NEW.user_name, receiver_id = receiver, type = msgType, question_id = qid, gmt_create = NEW.gmt_create;
	else
	  INSERT into t_message SET sender_id = new.user_id, sender_name = NEW.user_name, receiver_id = receiver, type = msgType, question_id = new.parent, gmt_create = NEW.gmt_create;
	end if;
  END IF;
END */;;

CREATE TABLE `t_question` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `type` int(11) NOT NULL COMMENT '问题名称',
  `content` text NOT NULL COMMENT '问题内容',
  `buyer_id` int(11) NOT NULL COMMENT '买家id',
  `user_name` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `user_logo` varchar(80) DEFAULT NULL,
  `cnt_PA` int(11) DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '专业回答数量',
  `cnt_CA` int(11) DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '普通回答数量',
  `state` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '0=已发布，1=草稿',
  `gmt_create` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00' COMMENT '记录创建时间',
  `gmt_modify` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '记录修改时间',
  `industry` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `process_method` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `wp_hardness` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `wp_material` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `has_pic` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=132 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COMMENT='刀具问题表';

CREATE TABLE `t_user` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `nick` varchar(50) DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'QQ connect 昵称',
  `mail` varchar(45) NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '登录密码',
  `company_name` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '公司名称',
  `brand` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `brand_name` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '代理品牌名称',
  `brand2` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `brand_name2` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '代理品牌名称',
  `logo` varchar(80) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '品牌logo',
  `address` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '公司地址',
  `phone` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '公司电话',
  `fax` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '公司传真',
  `description` varchar(2000) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '公司介绍',
  `authority` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `verified_link` varchar(80) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '证书链接',
  `contact_name` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '联系人名称',
  `contact_phone` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '联系人手机',
  `contact_qq` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '联系人QQ',
  `contact_email` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '联系人邮箱',
  `cnt_read` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `cnt_answer` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `cnt_sample` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `cnt_gc` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `productlimit` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '2',
  `pca` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reg_time` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00' COMMENT '注册时间',
  `gmt_create` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00' COMMENT '记录创建时间',
  `gmt_modified` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '记录修改时间(最近登录时间)',
  `gmt_auth` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `company_name` (`company_name`),
  KEY `nick` (`nick`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=421 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COMMENT='代理商表';
